<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E6%B6%88%E6%AD%A7%E4%B9%89" title="Wikipedia:消歧义"><img alt="Disambig gray.svg" data-file-height="168" data-file-width="220" decoding="async" height="19" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/25px-Disambig_gray.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/38px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/50px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 2x" width="25"/></a>  此條目介紹的是数学的复数。关于數學或统计学的众數，请见「<b><a href="/wiki/%E4%BC%97%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="众数 (数学)">众数 (数学)</a></b>」。关于语言学的复数或称众数，请见「<b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95)" title="复数 (语法)">复数 (语法)</a></b>」。</div>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle i={\sqrt {-{1}}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b13bc2b4f7e103e92342633692e46d585913f342" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.807ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span><br/>
<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7" title="无穷">無窮大</a> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \infty }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi mathvariant="normal">∞<!-- ∞ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \infty }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\infty" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c26c105004f30c27aa7c2a9c601550a4183b1f21" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.324ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>
</p>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td align="right"><div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:%E6%95%B8" title="Template:數"><abbr title="查看该模板">查</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:%E6%95%B8" title="Template talk:數"><abbr title="讨论该模板">论</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:%E6%95%B8&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="编辑该模板">编</abbr></a></li></ul></div>

<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Domain_coloring_x2-1_x-2-i_x-2-i_d_x2%2B2%2B2i.xcf"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Domain_coloring_x2-1_x-2-i_x-2-i_d_x2%2B2%2B2i.xcf/300px-Domain_coloring_x2-1_x-2-i_x-2-i_d_x2%2B2%2B2i.xcf.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Domain_coloring_x2-1_x-2-i_x-2-i_d_x2%2B2%2B2i.xcf/400px-Domain_coloring_x2-1_x-2-i_x-2-i_d_x2%2B2%2B2i.xcf.png 2x" width="200"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Domain_coloring_x2-1_x-2-i_x-2-i_d_x2%2B2%2B2i.xcf" title="放大"></a></div><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r72900767">.mw-parser-output .sfrac{white-space:nowrap}.mw-parser-output .sfrac.tion,.mw-parser-output .sfrac .tion{display:inline-block;vertical-align:-0.5em;font-size:85%;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .sfrac .num,.mw-parser-output .sfrac .den{display:block;line-height:1em;margin:0 0.1em}.mw-parser-output .sfrac .den{border-top:1px solid}.mw-parser-output .sr-only{border:0;clip:rect(0,0,0,0);height:1px;margin:-1px;overflow:hidden;padding:0;position:absolute;width:1px}</style><span class="sfrac tion" role="math"><span class="num">(<i>z</i><sup>2</sup> − 1)(<i>z</i> − 2 − <i>i</i>)<sup>2</sup></span><span class="sr-only">/</span><span class="den"><i>z</i><sup>2</sup> + 2 + 2<i>i</i></span></span></span></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E8%89%B2%E7%9B%B8%E7%92%B0%E8%A4%87%E8%AE%8A%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8%E5%9C%96%E5%BD%A2" title="色相環複變函數圖形">色相環複變函數圖形</a>。<a href="/wiki/%E8%89%B2%E7%9B%B8" title="色相">色相</a>表示函数的辐角，<a href="/wiki/%E8%89%B2%E5%BA%A6_(%E8%89%B2%E5%BD%A9%E5%AD%A6)" title="色度 (色彩学)">饱和度</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E6%98%8E%E5%BA%A6" title="明度">明度</a>表示函数的幅值。</div></div></div>
<p><b>複數</b>，為<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AF%A6%E6%95%B8" title="實數">實數</a>的延伸，它使任一<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E9%A0%85%E5%BC%8F" title="多項式">多項式</a><a href="/wiki/%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="方程">方程</a>都有<a href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B9_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="根 (数学)">根</a>。複數當中有個「<a href="/wiki/%E8%99%9B%E6%95%B8%E5%96%AE%E4%BD%8D" title="虛數單位">虛數單位</a>」<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle i}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>i</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle i}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="i" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/add78d8608ad86e54951b8c8bd6c8d8416533d20" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.802ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，它是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle -1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle -1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="-1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/704fb0427140d054dd267925495e78164fee9aac" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:2.971ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>的一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E6%A0%B9" title="平方根">平方根</a>，即<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {{i}^{2}}=-1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msup>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>i</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {{i}^{2}}=-1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {{i}^{2}}=-1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cab082841288a1395251d6d7ab06156bbd1dbee2" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:7.926ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。任一複數都可表達為<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x+yi}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>y</mi>
<mi>i</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x+yi}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x + yi" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c21e83615ab4f0b0dc3c3e8f285d92e82faf7095" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:6.128ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>，其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>及<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>y</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle y}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="y" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8a6208ec717213d4317e666f1ae872e00620a0d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.155ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>皆為實數，分別稱為複數之「實部」和「虛部」。
</p><p>複數的發現源於<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E6%AC%A1%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="三次方程">三次方程</a>的根的表達式。數學上，「複」字表明所討論的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E9%AB%94" title="數體">數體</a>為複數，如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%9F%A9%E9%99%A3" title="矩陣">複矩陣</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E5%8F%98%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="复变函数">複變函數</a>等。
</p><p>形式上，複數系統可以定義為普通實數的虛數i的<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%9F%E6%89%A9%E5%BC%A0" title="域扩张">代數擴展</a>。這意味著複數可以作為變量i中的多項式進行加，減和乘，並施加規則<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {{i}^{2}}=-1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msup>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>i</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {{i}^{2}}=-1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {{i}^{2}}=-1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cab082841288a1395251d6d7ab06156bbd1dbee2" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:7.926ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。此外，複數也可以除以非零複數。總體而言，複數系統是一個<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9F%9F_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="域 (數學)">域</a>。
</p><p>在幾何上，複數通過將水平軸用於實部，將垂直軸用於虛部，將<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E7%BB%B4" title="一维">一維</a><a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E7%B7%9A" title="數線">數線</a>的概念擴展到<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%8C%E7%B6%AD" title="二維">二維</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A4%87%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2" title="複平面">複平面</a>。這些數字的點位於複平面的垂直軸上。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%99%9B%E6%95%B8" title="虛數">虛部</a>為零的複數可以看作是實數。
</p><p>但是，複數允許使用更豐富的代數結構，其中包括在<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%91%E9%87%8F" title="向量">向量</a>空間中不一定可用的附加運算。例如，兩個複數的乘積總是再次產生一個複數，並且不應將其誤認為是涉及向量的常規“乘積”。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E6.AD.B7.E5.8F.B2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="歷史">歷史</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：歷史">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>最早提到有關<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B2%A0%E6%95%B8" title="負數">負數</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E6%A0%B9" title="平方根">平方根</a>的文獻出於公元1世紀<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%85%8A%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="古希腊数学">古希腊数学家</a><a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%9A%E5%8E%86%E5%B1%B1%E5%A4%A7%E6%B8%AF%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E7%BD%97" title="亚历山大港的希罗">亞歷山卓的希羅</a>，他考慮的是一種不可能的平頂金字塔的體積，計算結果會是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {81-144}}=3i{\sqrt {7}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mn>81</mn>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>144</mn>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mi>i</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mn>7</mn>
</msqrt>

</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mn>7</mn>
</msqrt>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {144-81}}=3{\sqrt {7}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {144-81}}=3{\sqrt {7}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/03d90aa56533469b14b5a9ac2fcc318bab0f4128" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:17.948ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p><p>16世紀意大利數學家（請參看<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A1%94%E5%A1%94%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%9A" title="塔塔利亚">塔塔利亞</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E5%B0%94%E8%BE%BE%E8%AF%BA" title="卡尔达诺">卡爾達諾</a>）得出<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E6%AC%A1%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="三次方程">一元三次</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%9B%E6%AC%A1%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="四次方程">四次方程式</a>的根的表達式，並發現即使只考慮實數根，仍不可避免面對負數方根。17世紀<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AC%9B%E5%8D%A1%E5%85%92" title="笛卡兒">笛卡兒</a>稱負數方根為<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%99%9B%E6%95%B8" title="虛數">虛數</a>，「子虛烏有的數」，表達對此的無奈和不忿。18世紀初<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A3%A3%E8%8E%AB%E5%BC%97" title="棣莫弗">棣莫弗</a>及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E6%8B%89" title="歐拉">歐拉</a>大力推動複數的接受。1730年，棣莫弗提出<a href="/wiki/%E6%A3%A3%E8%8E%AB%E5%BC%97%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="棣莫弗公式">棣莫弗公式</a>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (\cos \theta +i\sin \theta )^{n}=\cos n\theta +i\sin n\theta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<p>而歐拉則在1748年提出<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90%E5%AD%A6" title="分析学">分析學</a>中的<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="欧拉公式">歐拉公式</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \cos \theta +i\sin \theta =e^{i\theta }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>cos</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>θ<!-- θ --></mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>i</mi>
<mi>sin</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>θ<!-- θ --></mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>i</mi>
<mi>θ<!-- θ --></mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \cos \theta +i\sin \theta =e^{i\theta }}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\cos \theta +i\sin \theta =e^{{i\theta }}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7374fdde62826dbddd192da0534e3d87decdcacd" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:18.704ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，</dd></dl>
<p>18世紀末，複數漸漸被大多數人接受，當時<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E6%96%AF%E5%B8%95%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E9%9F%A6%E5%A1%9E%E5%B0%94" title="卡斯帕尔·韦塞尔">卡斯帕尔·韦塞尔</a>提出複數可看作平面上的一點。數年後，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF" title="高斯">高斯</a>再提出此觀點並大力推廣，複數的研究開始高速發展。詫異的是，早於1685年<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%84%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E6%B2%83%E5%88%A9%E6%96%AF_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%AE%B6)" title="約翰·沃利斯 (數學家)">約翰·沃利斯</a>已經在<i>De Algebra tractatus</i>提出此一觀點。
</p><p>卡斯帕尔·韦塞尔的文章發表在1799年的<i>Proceedings of the Copenhagen Academy</i>上，以當今標準來看，也是相當清楚和完備。他又考慮<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%90%83%E9%AB%94" title="球體">球体</a>，得出<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%9B%E5%85%83%E6%95%B8" title="四元數">四元數</a>並以此提出完備的<a href="/wiki/%E7%90%83%E9%9D%A2%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%AD%B8" title="球面三角學">球面三角學</a>理論。1804年，Abbé Buée亦獨立地提出與沃利斯相似的觀點，即以<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pm {\sqrt {-1}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>±<!-- ± --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pm {\sqrt {-1}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pm {\sqrt  {-1}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3b6895558c83e7bfb958447c4b5e0a001f772867" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.715ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>來表示平面上與實數軸垂直的單位線段。1806年，Buée的文章正式刊出，同年<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%93-%E7%BE%85%E8%B2%9D%E7%88%BE%C2%B7%E9%98%BF%E7%88%BE%E5%B2%A1" title="讓-羅貝爾·阿爾岡">讓-羅貝爾·阿爾岡</a>亦發表同類文章，而阿岡的複數平面成了標準。1831年高斯認為複數不夠普及，次年他發表了一篇備忘錄，奠定複數在數學的地位。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF" title="柯西">柯西</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BC%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E9%98%BF%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94" title="尼尔斯·阿贝尔">阿贝尔</a>的努力，掃除了複數使用的最後顧忌，後者更是首位以複數研究著名的。
</p><p>複數吸引了著名<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%AE%B6" title="數學家">數學家</a>的注意，包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BA%93%E9%BB%98%E5%B0%94" title="库默尔">库默尔</a>（1844年）、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%8B%E7%BD%97%E5%86%85%E5%85%8B" title="克罗内克">克罗内克</a>（1845年）、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Scheffler&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Scheffler（页面不存在）">Scheffler</a>（1845年、1851年、1880年）、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Bellavitis&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Bellavitis（页面不存在）">Bellavitis</a>（1835年、1852年）、<a href="/wiki/%E5%96%AC%E6%B2%BB%C2%B7%E7%9A%AE%E7%A7%91%E5%85%8B" title="喬治·皮科克">喬治·皮科克</a>（1845年）及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E6%91%A9%E6%A0%B9" title="德·摩根">德·摩根</a>（1849年）。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8E%AB%E6%AF%94%E4%B9%8C%E6%96%AF" title="莫比乌斯">莫比乌斯</a>發表了大量有關複數幾何的短文，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%84%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E5%BD%BC%E5%BE%97%C2%B7%E7%8B%84%E5%88%A9%E5%85%8B%E9%9B%B7" title="約翰·彼得·狄利克雷">約翰·彼得·狄利克雷</a>將很多實數概念，例如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8" title="質數">質數</a>，推廣至複數。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E8%B2%BB%E8%BF%AA%E5%8D%97%C2%B7%E8%89%BE%E6%A3%AE%E6%96%AF%E5%9D%A6" title="費迪南·艾森斯坦">費迪南·艾森斯坦</a>研究<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a+bj}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mi>j</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a+bj}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a+bj" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6e0624a5ff286b08713c4b828fadadfac9fff1c5" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:6.026ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>，其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle j}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="j" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2f461e54f5c093e92a55547b9764291390f0b5d0" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.027ex; width:0.985ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x^{3}-1=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x^{3}-1=0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c20206a9bf6ccbe5e90a69a37b0f1f33ff34e8b8" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:10.648ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>的複根。其他如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x^{k}-1=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x^{k}-1=0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/37fbda08853fb710773a29c10ab69105633509bc" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:10.682ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> (<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle k}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="k" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3c9a2c7b599b37105512c5d570edc034056dd40" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.211ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>是質數)亦有考慮。類以推廣的先鋒為库默尔的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8C%E7%BE%8E%E6%95%B8" title="完美數">完美數</a>理論，經由<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8F%B2%E5%88%A9%E5%85%8B%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E5%85%8B%E8%8E%B1%E5%9B%A0" title="菲利克斯·克莱因">菲利克斯·克莱因</a>（1893年）以幾何角度加以簡化。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BC%BD%E7%BD%97%E5%8D%8E" title="伽罗华">伽羅華</a>其後提出更一般的推廣，解決了五次以上多項式的根不能表達問題。
</p><p><br/>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E7.BE.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定義">定義</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：定義">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E7.AC.A6.E5.8F.B7.E8.A1.A8.E7.A4.BA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="符号表示">符号表示</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：符号表示">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>尽管可以使用其他表示法，复数通常写为如下形式：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a+bi}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mi>i</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a+bi}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a+bi" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a92f853c2c9235c06be640b91b7c75e2a907cbda" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:5.87ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>这裡的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>是<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0" title="实数">实数</a>，而<i>i</i>是<a href="/wiki/%E8%99%9B%E6%95%B8%E5%96%AE%E4%BD%8D" title="虛數單位">虛數單位</a>，它有着性质<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {{i}^{2}}=-1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msup>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>i</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {{i}^{2}}=-1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {{i}^{2}}=-1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cab082841288a1395251d6d7ab06156bbd1dbee2" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:7.926ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。实数<b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></b>叫做复数的<b>实部</b>，而实数<b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span></b>叫做复数的<b>虚部</b>。实数可以被认为是虚部为零的复数；就是说实数<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</semantics>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mn>0</mn>
<mi>i</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

</p><p>例如，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 3+2i}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>所有复数的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="集合 (数学)">集合</a>通常指示为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>C</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

<semantics>

</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.AD.89.E9.87.8F.E5.85.B3.E7.B3.BB"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="等量关系">等量关系</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：等量关系">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>复数中的虚数是无法比较大小的，即两个虚数只有相等和不等两种等量关系。
</p><p>两个复数是相等的，<a href="/wiki/%E5%BD%93%E4%B8%94%E4%BB%85%E5%BD%93" title="当且仅当">当且仅当</a>它们的实部是相等的并且它们的虚部是相等的。就是说，設<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>,<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>,<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle c}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>c</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle c}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="c" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/86a67b81c2de995bd608d5b2df50cd8cd7d92455" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.007ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>,<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle d}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>d</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle d}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="d" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e85ff03cbe0c7341af6b982e47e9f90d235c66ab" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.216ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>為實數，則<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a+bi=c+di}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mi>i</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>c</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>d</mi>
<mi>i</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a+bi=c+di}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle a+bi=c+di}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7779531f65f6ca1cbb12f3beae22e7716f583ba1" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:14.834ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>当且仅当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a=c}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>c</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a=c}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle a=c}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1beb3f1b1ad87e99791ba713839204a88b27239a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.335ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>并且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b=d}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>d</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b=d}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle b=d}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d313b2b19adc53ca61b0af421d36cdb04e8507b7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.312ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.BF.90.E7.AE.97"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="运算">运算</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：运算">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>通过形式上应用<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0" title="代数">代数</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E7%BB%93%E5%90%88%E5%BE%8B" title="结合律">结合律</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E6%8D%A2%E5%BE%8B" title="交换律">交换律</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E9%85%8D%E5%BE%8B" title="分配律">分配律</a>，再加上等式<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {{i}^{2}}=-1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mo>=</mo>

<h3><span id=".E8.A4.87.E6.95.B8.E9.AB.94"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="複數體">複數體</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：複數體">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>複數可定義為實數<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a,b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a,b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a, b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/181523deba732fda302fd176275a0739121d3bc8" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.261ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>組成的<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E5%BA%8F%E5%AF%B9" title="有序对">有序對</a>，而其相關之<a href="/wiki/%E5%8A%A0%E6%B3%95" title="加法">和</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E7%A7%AF" title="积">積</a>為：
</p>
<ul><li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (a,b)+(c,d)=(a+c,b+d)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>

<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>c</mi>

<mo>+</mo>

<mo>+</mo>
<mi>d</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (a,b)+(c,d)=(a+c,b+d)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="(a,b)+(c,d)=(a+c,b+d)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a427192a7477dd41aa915f664310d2189676175e" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:29.05ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，</li></ul>
<ul><li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (a,b)\cdot (c,d)=(ac-bd,bc+ad)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>複數數系是一個<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%9F_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="域 (数学)">體</a>，複數體常以<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">C</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbb {C} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f9add4085095b9b6d28d045fd9c92c2c09f549a7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>來表示。
</p><p>一個實數<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>

</p>

<p>複數體亦可定為<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8%E6%95%B8" title="代數數">代數數</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%8B%93%E6%89%91%E9%97%AD%E5%8C%85" title="拓扑闭包">拓撲閉包</a>或實數體的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8%E9%96%89%E5%8C%85" title="代數閉包">代數閉包</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.A4.87.E6.95.B8.E5.B9.B3.E9.9D.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="複數平面">複數平面</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：複數平面">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2" title="复数平面">複數平面</a></div>
<p>先把坐标轴画出来，横的叫实轴，竖的叫虚轴，然后确定0的位置，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z=a+bi}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>z</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mi>i</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z=a+bi}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="z=a+bi" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/eef52538a0077e8dff45f937a232364d68ca6124" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:10.057ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>可以用二维空间来表示出来。<br/>
复数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>z</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="z" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf368e72c009decd9b6686ee84a375632e11de98" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.088ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>可以被看作在被称为<b>阿甘得图</b>（得名於<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%AE%A9-%E7%BD%97%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E9%98%BF%E5%86%88" title="让-罗贝尔·阿冈">让-罗贝尔·阿冈</a>，也叫做<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF" title="高斯">高斯</a>平面）的二维<a href="/wiki/%E7%AC%9B%E5%8D%A1%E5%B0%94%E5%9D%90%E6%A0%87%E7%B3%BB" title="笛卡尔坐标系">笛卡尔坐标系</a>内的一个点或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%9F%A2%E9%87%8F" title="矢量">位置向量</a>。这个点也就是这个复数<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>z</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="z" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf368e72c009decd9b6686ee84a375632e11de98" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.088ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></i>可以用笛卡尔（直角）坐标指定。复数的笛卡尔坐标是实部<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x=\Re z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi mathvariant="normal">ℜ<!-- ℜ --></mi>
<mi>z</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x=\Re z}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle x=\Re z}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/567dd4d67d897fb26a45a3bc114ce0659fb43f60" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.441ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>和虚部<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y=\Im z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>y</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi mathvariant="normal">ℑ<!-- ℑ --></mi>
<mi>z</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle y=\Im z}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle y=\Im z}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0519e03af896ccf432a8d6cb59844b2d87849680" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:6.63ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>。复数的笛卡尔坐标表示叫做复数的“笛卡尔形式”、“直角形式”或“代数形式”。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.B5.95.E5.B0.8D.E5.80.BC.E3.80.81.E5.85.B1.E8.BB.9B.E8.88.87.E8.B7.9D.E9.9B.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="絕對值、共軛與距離">絕對值、共軛與距離</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：絕對值、共軛與距離">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z=re^{i\phi }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>z</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>r</mi>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>i</mi>
<mi>ϕ<!-- ϕ --></mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z=re^{i\phi }}</annotation>
</semantics>

<p>當定義了距離<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle d(z,w)=\left|z-w\right|}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>對於所有代數運算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>，共軛值是可交換的。這即是說<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f({\overline {z}})={\overline {f(z)}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mover>

<mo>=</mo>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f({\overline {z}})={\overline {f(z)}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(\overline z)=\overline {f(z)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/64a9e05ae3a4b24dd6414f35fbd76c7e3e087894" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:11.685ex; height:3.676ex;"/></span>。一些非代數運算如<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%BC%A6" title="正弦">正弦</a>「<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sin }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>一複數<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z=re^{i\phi }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>對於乘法和除法分別有：

<h3><span id=".E5.A4.8D.E6.95.B0.E8.BF.90.E7.AE.97.E7.9A.84.E5.87.A0.E4.BD.95.E8.A7.A3.E9.87.8A"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="复数运算的几何解释">复数运算的几何解释</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：复数运算的几何解释">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Complex_numbers_addition.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="473" data-file-width="468" decoding="async" height="222" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Complex_numbers_addition.png/220px-Complex_numbers_addition.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Complex_numbers_addition.png/330px-Complex_numbers_addition.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Complex_numbers_addition.png/440px-Complex_numbers_addition.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Complex_numbers_addition.png" title="放大"></a></div><i>X</i> = <i>A</i> + <i>B</i></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Complex_numbers_multiplication.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="180" data-file-width="242" decoding="async" height="164" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/Complex_numbers_multiplication.png/220px-Complex_numbers_multiplication.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/a/ac/Complex_numbers_multiplication.png 1.5x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Complex_numbers_multiplication.png" title="放大"></a></div><i>X</i> = <i>AB</i></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Complex_numbers_conjugation.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="238" data-file-width="236" decoding="async" height="222" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Complex_numbers_conjugation.png/220px-Complex_numbers_conjugation.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/04/Complex_numbers_conjugation.png 1.5x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Complex_numbers_conjugation.png" title="放大"></a></div><i>X</i> = <i>A</i>*</div></div></div>
<p>考虑一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="平面 (数学)">平面</a>。一个点是原点0。另一个点是单位1。
</p><p>两个点<i>A</i>和<i>B</i>的<b>和</b>是点<i>X</i> = <i>A</i> + <i>B</i>使得<a href="/wiki/%E9%A0%82%E9%BB%9E_(%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95)" title="頂點 (幾何)">顶点</a>0, <i>A</i>, <i>B</i>的<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%BD%A2" title="三角形">三角形</a>和顶点<i>A</i>, <i>B</i>, <i>X</i>的三角形是<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E7%AD%89" title="全等">全等</a>的。
</p><p>两个点<i>A</i>和<i>B</i>的<b>积</b>是点<i>X</i> = <i>AB</i>使得顶点0, 1, <i>A</i>的三角形和顶点<i>0</i>, <i>B</i>, <i>X</i>的三角形是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B8%E4%BC%BC" title="相似">相似</a>的。
</p><p>点<i>A</i>的<b>共轭复数</b>是点<i>X</i> = <i>A</i><sup>*</sup>使得顶点0, 1, <i>A</i>的三角形和顶点0, 1, <i>X</i>的三角形相互是<a href="/wiki/%E9%95%9C%E5%83%8F_(%E5%87%A0%E4%BD%95)" title="镜像 (几何)">镜像</a>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.9E.81.E5.9D.90.E6.A0.87.E5.BD.A2.E5.BC.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="极坐标形式">极坐标形式</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：极坐标形式">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>作为替代，复数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.BB.8E.E6.9E.81.E5.9D.90.E6.A0.87.E5.BD.A2.E5.BC.8F.E5.88.B0.E7.AC.9B.E5.8D.A1.E5.B0.94.E5.9D.90.E6.A0.87.E5.BD.A2.E5.BC.8F.E7.9A.84.E8.BD.AC.E6.8D.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="从极坐标形式到笛卡尔坐标形式的转换">从极坐标形式到笛卡尔坐标形式的转换</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：从极坐标形式到笛卡尔坐标形式的转换">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span id=".E4.BB.8E.E7.AC.9B.E5.8D.A1.E5.B0.94.E5.9D.90.E6.A0.87.E5.BD.A2.E5.BC.8F.E5.88.B0.E6.9E.81.E5.9D.90.E6.A0.87.E5.BD.A2.E5.BC.8F.E7.9A.84.E8.BD.AC.E6.8D.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="从笛卡尔坐标形式到极坐标形式的转换">从笛卡尔坐标形式到极坐标形式的转换</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：从笛卡尔坐标形式到极坐标形式的转换">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle r={\sqrt {x^{2}+y^{2}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \varphi ={\begin{cases}\arctan({\frac {y}{x}})&amp;{\mbox{if }}x&gt;0\\\arctan({\frac {y}{x}})+\pi &amp;{\mbox{if }}x&lt;0{\mbox{ and }}y\geq 0\\\arctan({\frac {y}{x}})-\pi &amp;{\mbox{if }}x&lt;0{\mbox{ and }}y&lt;0\\+{\frac {\pi }{2}}&amp;{\mbox{if }}x=0{\mbox{ and }}y&gt;0\\-{\frac {\pi }{2}}&amp;{\mbox{if }}x=0{\mbox{ and }}y&lt;0\\\mathrm {undefined} &amp;{\mbox{if }}x=0{\mbox{ and }}y=0.\end{cases}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\varphi ={\begin{cases}\arctan({\frac  {y}{x}})&amp;{\mbox{if }}x&gt;0\\\arctan({\frac  {y}{x}})+\pi &amp;{\mbox{if }}x&lt;0{\mbox{ and }}y\geq 0\\\arctan({\frac  {y}{x}})-\pi &amp;{\mbox{if }}x&lt;0{\mbox{ and }}y&lt;0\\+{\frac  {\pi }{2}}&amp;{\mbox{if }}x=0{\mbox{ and }}y&gt;0\\-{\frac  {\pi }{2}}&amp;{\mbox{if }}x=0{\mbox{ and }}y&lt;0\\{\mathrm  {undefined}}&amp;{\mbox{if }}x=0{\mbox{ and }}y=0.\end{cases}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9648bf9749521b0e9121338ac7840c24c7e258fb" style="vertical-align: -8.956ex; margin-bottom: -0.215ex; width:42.485ex; height:19.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>前面的公式要求非常繁杂的情况区分。但是很多编程语言提供了经常叫做<a href="/wiki/Atan2" title="Atan2">atan2</a>一个变体的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E6%AD%A3%E5%88%87" title="反正切">反正切</a>函数来处理这些细节。使用反余弦函数的公式要求更少的情况区分:
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \varphi ={\begin{cases}+\arccos {\frac {x}{r}}&amp;{\mbox{if }}y\geq 0{\mbox{ and }}r\neq 0\\-\arccos {\frac {x}{r}}&amp;{\mbox{if }}y&lt;0\\\mathrm {undefined} &amp;{\mbox{if }}r=0.\end{cases}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E6.9E.81.E5.9D.90.E6.A0.87.E5.BD.A2.E5.BC.8F.E7.9A.84.E7.AC.A6.E5.8F.B7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="极坐标形式的符号">极坐标形式的符号</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：极坐标形式的符号">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>极坐标形式的符号
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z=r\,(\cos \varphi +i\sin \varphi )}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>z</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>r</mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>cos</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>φ<!-- φ --></mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>i</mi>
<mi>sin</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>φ<!-- φ --></mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z=r\,(\cos \varphi +i\sin \varphi )}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="z=r\,(\cos \varphi +i\sin \varphi )" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6bfe0b1c41ac1be227f47728feaa2f966aca3ffa" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:21.243ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，</dd></dl>
<p>被叫做“三角形式”。有时使用符号<a href="/wiki/Cis%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="Cis函數">cis</a> φ简写<a href="/wiki/%E9%A4%98%E5%BC%A6" title="餘弦"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">c</span>os</a>φ + <span style="text-decoration: underline;"><i>i</i></span><a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%BC%A6" title="正弦"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">s</span>in</a>φ。
使用<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="欧拉公式">欧拉公式</a>还可以写为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z=r\,\mathrm {e} ^{i\varphi }\,,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>z</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>r</mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<msup>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>i</mi>
<mi>φ<!-- φ --></mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mo>,</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z=r\,\mathrm {e} ^{i\varphi }\,,}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="z=r\,{\mathrm  {e}}^{{i\varphi }}\,," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ee48d08607eb54591f8792a69fb6abafee261ba5" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:9.563ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>这叫做“指数形式”。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.9E.81.E5.9D.90.E6.A0.87.E5.BD.A2.E5.BC.8F.E4.B8.8B.E7.9A.84.E4.B9.98.E6.B3.95.E3.80.81.E9.99.A4.E6.B3.95.E3.80.81.E6.8C.87.E6.95.B0.E5.92.8C.E5.BC.80.E6.96.B9.E6.A0.B9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="极坐标形式下的乘法、除法、指数和开方根">极坐标形式下的乘法、除法、指数和开方根</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：极坐标形式下的乘法、除法、指数和开方根">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>在极坐标形式下乘法、除法、指数和开方根要比笛卡尔形式下容易许多。
</p><p>使用<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E6%81%92%E7%AD%89%E5%BC%8F#角的和差恒等式" title="三角恒等式">三角恒等式</a>得到
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle r_{1}\,e^{i\varphi _{1}}\cdot r_{2}\,e^{i\varphi _{2}}=r_{1}\,r_{2}\,e^{i(\varphi _{1}+\varphi _{2})}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {r_{1}\,e^{i\varphi _{1}}}{r_{2}\,e^{i\varphi _{2}}}}={\frac {r_{1}}{r_{2}}}\,e^{i(\varphi _{1}-\varphi _{2})}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\frac  {r_{1}\,e^{{i\varphi _{1}}}}{r_{2}\,e^{{i\varphi _{2}}}}}={\frac  {r_{1}}{r_{2}}}\,e^{{i(\varphi _{1}-\varphi _{2})}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4de23b2d6decd22d31fc54498ebc2fd95182e83f" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:21.794ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>依据<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A3%A3%E8%8E%AB%E5%BC%97%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="棣莫弗定理">棣莫弗定理</a>做整数幂的指数运算，
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\big (}r\,e^{i\varphi }{\big )}^{n}=r^{n}\,e^{in\varphi }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\big (}r\,e^{i\varphi }{\big )}^{n}=r^{n}\,e^{in\varphi }}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\big (}r\,e^{{i\varphi }}{\big )}^{n}=r^{n}\,e^{{in\varphi }}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9818e8a820eb2ce384c484fa4daba676a6314b44" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:17.439ex; height:3.343ex;"/></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>任意复数幂的指数运算在条目<a href="/wiki/%E6%8C%87%E6%95%B0%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="指数函数">指数函数</a>中讨论。
</p><p>两个复数的加法只是两个向量的<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%91%E9%87%8F%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="向量空间">向量加法</a>，乘以一个固定复数的可以被看作同时旋转和伸缩。
</p><p>乘以<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle i}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>i</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle i}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="i" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/add78d8608ad86e54951b8c8bd6c8d8416533d20" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.802ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>对应于一个逆时针旋转90 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A7%92%E5%BA%A6" title="角度">度</a>(<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {\pi }{2}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mn>2</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {\pi }{2}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\frac{\pi}{2}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/98f98bef5d4981ff6e2aa827d4699e347fb30db2" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:2.168ex; height:4.676ex;"/></span> <a href="/wiki/%E5%BC%A7%E5%BA%A6" title="弧度">弧度</a>)。方程<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle i^{2}=-1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle i^{2}=-1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="i^{2}=-1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/88e98a401d352e5037d5043028e2d7f449e83fa6" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:7.926ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>的几何意义是顺序的两个90度旋转导致一个180度(<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>弧度)旋转。甚至算术中的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (-1)\times (-1)=+1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>

<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo>+</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (-1)\times (-1)=+1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3fd9a3159b067cf7c7dee6afd85f77a1f35fabdb" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:18.469ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>都可以被在几何上被理解为两个180度旋转的组合。
</p><p>任何数的所有<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%B9%E6%A0%B9" title="方根">方根</a>，实数或复数的，都可以用简单的<a href="/wiki/%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="算法">算法</a>找到。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>

<p>对于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle k=0,1,2,\ldots ,n-1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h2><span id=".E4.BB.A3.E6.95.B8.E6.80.A7.E8.B3.AA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="代數性質"><a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0" title="代数">代數</a>性質</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：代數性質">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span id=".E4.B8.80.E4.BA.9B.E7.89.B9.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="一些特性">一些特性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="编辑章节：一些特性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E7.9F.A9.E9.99.A3.E8.A1.A8.E9.81.94.E5.BC.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="矩陣表達式">矩陣表達式</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="编辑章节：矩陣表達式">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>這是個實用價值不大，但具數學意義的表達式，是將複數看作能<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%8B%E8%BD%89" title="旋轉">旋轉</a>及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B8%AE%E6%94%BE" title="縮放">縮放</a>二維位置矢量的2×2實數<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%9F%A9%E9%99%A3" title="矩陣">矩陣</a>，即是
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a+ib\leftrightarrow {\begin{pmatrix}a&amp;-b\\b&amp;\;\;a\end{pmatrix}}=r{\begin{bmatrix}\cos \varphi &amp;-\sin \varphi \\\sin \varphi &amp;\cos \varphi \end{bmatrix}}=r\exp \left(\varphi {\begin{bmatrix}0&amp;-1\\1&amp;0\end{bmatrix}}\right),}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{pmatrix}a&amp;-b\\b&amp;\;\;a\end{pmatrix}}=a{\begin{pmatrix}1&amp;\;\;0\\0&amp;\;\;1\end{pmatrix}}+b{\begin{pmatrix}0&amp;-1\\1&amp;\;\;0\end{pmatrix}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>即實數1對應着單位矩陣
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{pmatrix}1&amp;\;\;0\\0&amp;\;\;1\end{pmatrix}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="{\begin{pmatrix}1&amp;\;\;0\\0&amp;\;\;1\end{pmatrix}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e4b98f33aeb4fc1f7f70a928bfafe296c5fbacda" style="vertical-align: -2.505ex; width:10.11ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span>，</dd></dl>
<p>而虛數單位<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle i}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>i</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle i}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="i" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/add78d8608ad86e54951b8c8bd6c8d8416533d20" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.802ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>對應着
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{pmatrix}0&amp;-1\\1&amp;\;\;0\end{pmatrix}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow>
<mo>(</mo>
<mtable columnspacing="1em" rowspacing="4pt">
<mtr>
<mtd>
<mn>0</mn>
</mtd>
<mtd>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mtd>
</mtr>
<mtr>
<mtd>
<mn>1</mn>
</mtd>
<mtd>
<mspace width="thickmathspace"></mspace>
<mspace width="thickmathspace"></mspace>
<mn>0</mn>
</mtd>
</mtr>
</mtable>
<mo>)</mo>
</mrow>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\begin{pmatrix}0&amp;-1\\1&amp;\;\;0\end{pmatrix}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\begin{pmatrix}0&amp;-1\\1&amp;\;\;0\end{pmatrix}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/812b106352f0a46b36f60f29e6e38d3210649fec" style="vertical-align: -2.505ex; width:10.628ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span>。</dd></dl>
<p>此矩陣令平面作逆時鐘90度旋轉，它的平方就是-1。
</p><p>複數的絶對值就是<a href="/wiki/%E8%A1%8C%E5%88%97%E5%BC%8F" title="行列式">行列式</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E6%A0%B9" title="平方根">平方根</a>。這些矩陣對應相應的平面變換，其旋轉角度等於複數的徧角，改變比例等於複數的絶對值。複數的軛就是矩陣的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BD%89%E7%BD%AE" title="轉置">轉置</a>。
</p><p>若矩陣中的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>本來就是複數，則構成的代數便是<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%9B%E5%85%83%E6%95%B8" title="四元數">四元數</a>。由此，矩陣代表法可看成代數的<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%AF%E8%8E%B1-%E8%BF%AA%E5%85%8B%E6%A3%AE%E7%BB%93%E6%9E%84" title="凯莱-迪克森结构">凱萊-迪克森結構法</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.AF.A6.E5.90.91.E9.87.8F.E7.A9.BA.E9.96.93"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="實向量空間">實向量空間</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="编辑章节：實向量空間">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">C</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbb {C} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f9add4085095b9b6d28d045fd9c92c2c09f549a7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>可以視作二維<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AF%A6%E6%95%B8" title="實數">實</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BA%BF%E6%80%A7%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="线性空间">綫性空間</a>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup>不同於實數體，複數體上不可能有與其算術相容的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E5%BA%8F" title="全序">全序</a>：<b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">C</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbb {C} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f9add4085095b9b6d28d045fd9c92c2c09f549a7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span></b>並非<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E5%BA%8F%E9%AB%94" title="有序體">有序體</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.A4.9A.E9.A0.85.E5.BC.8F.E7.9A.84.E6.A0.B9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="多項式的根">多項式的根</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="编辑章节：多項式的根">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>滿足<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p(z)=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>p</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>z</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p(z)=0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle p(z)=0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/792ef81dfd42bba626d4ddf2589b28ecbb0e4f85" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:8.417ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>的複數<i>z</i>是<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E9%A0%85%E5%BC%8F" title="多項式">多項式</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>的“根”。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="代數基本定理">代數基本定理</a>指出，所有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>次多項式，不管實數系數抑或複數系數的，都剛好有<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>k</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle k}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="k" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3c9a2c7b599b37105512c5d570edc034056dd40" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.211ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>重根按<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle k}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="k" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3c9a2c7b599b37105512c5d570edc034056dd40" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.211ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span></i>个计算）。這定理等價於複數體是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8%E9%96%89%E9%AB%94" title="代數閉體">代數閉體</a>。
</p><p>事實上，複數體是實數體的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8%E9%96%89%E5%8C%85" title="代數閉包">代數閉包</a>。它是<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E9%A0%85%E5%BC%8F" title="多項式">多項式</a><a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%AF_(%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0)" title="环 (代数)">環</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} [X]}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
