</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.BB.A3.E6.95.B8.E7.89.B9.E5.BE.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="代數特徵">代數特徵</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="编辑章节：代數特徵">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>複數體<b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">C</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbb {C} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f9add4085095b9b6d28d045fd9c92c2c09f549a7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span></b>唯一（就<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%AB%94%E5%90%8C%E6%A7%8B&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="體同構（页面不存在）">體同構</a>來說）的體擁有三項代數特征:
</p>
<ul><li>它的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%E5%80%BC" title="特征值">特徵值</a>是0</li>
<li>它對<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E9%AB%94&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="質數體（页面不存在）">質數體</a>的<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B6%85%E8%B6%8A%E5%BA%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="超越度（页面不存在）">超越度</a>是<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD%E7%BB%9F" title="连续统">實數的基數</a></li>
<li>它是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8%E9%96%89%E5%8C%85" title="代數閉包">代數閉</a>的</li></ul>
<p>而然，<b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">C</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbb {C} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f9add4085095b9b6d28d045fd9c92c2c09f549a7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span></b>包含很多與<b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">C</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbb {C} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f9add4085095b9b6d28d045fd9c92c2c09f549a7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span></b>同構的子<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BD%93_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="体 (数学)">體</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.B8.8D.E5.8F.AF.E6.8E.92.E5.BA.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="不可排序">不可排序</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="编辑章节：不可排序">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>在<b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">C</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {C} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbb {C} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f9add4085095b9b6d28d045fd9c92c2c09f549a7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span></b>上不可能建立與其加法及乘法相容之<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E5%BA%8F%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB" title="全序关系">全序關係</a>，即不存在一全序<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \preceq }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.A4.8D.E6.8C.87.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="复指数幂">复指数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="编辑章节：复指数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%82#正实数的复数幂" title="幂">幂 § 正实数的复数幂</a></div>
<p>计算一个实数的复数幂是可以的。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{z}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>z</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{z}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^z" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6fda5d4b98ad1b1ded1a08a12990ef6f0e40316b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.231ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>可以定义为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e^{z\cdot \ln(a)}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<msup>

<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e^{z\cdot \ln(a)}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e^{z\cdot \ln(a)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4a067845a08975dc582d3633b663f7e7c7ae023b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.063ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E8.A4.87.E5.88.86.E6.9E.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="複分析">複分析</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="编辑章节：複分析">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>研究複變函數的理論稱為<a href="/wiki/%E8%A4%87%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="複分析">複分析</a>。它在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%87%89%E7%94%A8%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8" title="應用數學">應用數學</a>和其他數學分支上都有許多實際應用。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AF%A6%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="實分析">實分析</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E8%AB%96" title="數論">數論</a>的結果，最自然的證明經常是以複分析的技巧完成（例子可見<a href="/wiki/%E8%B3%AA%E6%95%B8%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="質數定理">質數定理</a>）。
</p><p>複變函數的圖像是四維的，所以不像實變函數般可以用平面圖像表示。要表示複變函數的圖像，可以用有顏色的三維圖像表達四維資訊，或者以動畫表示函數對複平面的動態變換。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.87.89.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="應用">應用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="编辑章节：應用">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E7.B3.BB.E7.BB.9F.E5.88.86.E6.9E.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="系统分析">系统分析</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="编辑章节：系统分析">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>在<a href="/wiki/%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="系统分析">系统分析</a>中，系统常常通过<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%89%E6%99%AE%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF%E5%8F%98%E6%8D%A2" title="拉普拉斯变换">拉普拉斯变换</a>从<a href="/wiki/%E6%99%82%E5%9F%9F" title="時域">时域</a>变换到<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A2%91%E5%9F%9F" title="频域">频域</a>。因此可在複平面上分析系统的<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E7%82%B9_(%E5%A4%8D%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90)" title="极点 (复分析)">极点</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%B6%E7%82%B9" title="零点">零点</a>。分析系统稳定性的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B9%E8%BD%A8%E8%BF%B9" title="根轨迹">根轨迹法</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%A5%88%E5%A5%8E%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%9B%BE" title="奈奎斯特图">奈奎斯特图法</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BC%E7%A7%91%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF%E5%9B%BE" title="尼科尔斯图">尼科尔斯图法</a>都是在複平面上进行的。
</p><p>无论系统极点和零点在左半平面还是右半平面，根轨迹法都很重要。如果系统极点
</p>
<ul><li>位于右半平面，则<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%A0%E6%9E%9C%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F" title="因果系统">因果系统</a>不稳定；</li>
<li>都位于左半平面，则因果系统稳定；</li>
<li>位于虚轴上，则系统为<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%A8%E7%95%8C%E7%A9%A9%E5%AE%9A" title="臨界穩定">临界稳定</a>的。</li></ul>
<p>如果稳定系统的全部零点都位于左半平面，则这是个<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9C%80%E5%B0%8F%E7%9B%B8%E4%BD%8D%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="最小相位系统（页面不存在）">最小相位系统</a>。如果系统的极点和零点关于虚轴对称，则这是<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%85%A8%E9%80%9A%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="全通系统（页面不存在）">全通系统</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.BF.A1.E5.8F.B7.E5.88.86.E6.9E.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="信号分析">信号分析</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="编辑章节：信号分析">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E5%8F%B7%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="信号分析（页面不存在）">信号分析</a>和其他领域使用复数可以方便的表示周期信号。模值<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left\vert z\right\vert }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow>
<mo>|</mo>
<mi>z</mi>
<mo>|</mo>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \left\vert z\right\vert }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \left\vert z\right\vert }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e09d238ddf8dd3a23b8355dccaf1b6fe1b39a68a" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:2.382ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>表示信号的<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B9%85%E5%BA%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="幅度（页面不存在）">幅度</a>，辐角<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \arg z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>arg</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>z</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \arg z}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \arg z}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3b42890eec05c72e9d06b055e4f5d0587f07067a" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:4.712ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>表示给定<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A2%91%E7%8E%87" title="频率">频率</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%BC%A6" title="正弦">正弦波</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B8%E4%BD%8D" title="相位">相位</a>。
</p><p>利用<a href="/wiki/%E5%82%85%E9%87%8C%E5%8F%B6%E5%8F%98%E6%8D%A2" title="傅里叶变换">傅里叶变换</a>可将实信号表示成一系列周期函数的和。这些周期函数通常用形式如下的複函數的实部表示：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(t)=ze^{i\omega t}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>t</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>z</mi>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>i</mi>
<mi>ω<!-- ω --></mi>
<mi>t</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(t)=ze^{i\omega t}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(t)=ze^{{i\omega t}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4830fcdd3f30e60add15ce80bef0f2388c7f6f0b" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:11.613ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>，</dd></dl>
<p>其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \omega }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>ω<!-- ω --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \omega }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\omega " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/48eff443f9de7a985bb94ca3bde20813ea737be8" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.446ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>对应<a href="/wiki/%E8%A7%92%E9%A2%91%E7%8E%87" title="角频率">角频率</a>，复数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>z</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="z" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf368e72c009decd9b6686ee84a375632e11de98" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.088ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>包含了幅度和相位的信息。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E8%B7%AF" title="电路">电路</a>分析中，引入<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E5%AE%B9" title="电容">电容</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E6%84%9F" title="电感">电感</a>与频率有关的虚部可以方便的将<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E5%8E%8B" title="电压">电压</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E6%B5%81" title="电流">电流</a>的关系用简单的线性方程表示并求解。（有时用字母<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle j}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>j</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle j}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="j" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2f461e54f5c093e92a55547b9764291390f0b5d0" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.027ex; width:0.985ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>作为虚数单位，以免与电流符号<i>i</i>混淆。）
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.8F.8D.E5.B8.B8.E7.A9.8D.E5.88.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="反常積分">反常積分</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="编辑章节：反常積分">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>在應用層面，複分析常用以計算某些實值的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E5%B8%B8%E7%A9%8D%E5%88%86" title="反常積分">反常積分</a>，藉由複值函數得出。方法有多種，見<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Methods of contour integration" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="圍道積分方法"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%8D%E9%81%93%E7%A9%8D%E5%88%86%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="圍道積分方法（页面不存在）">圍道積分方法</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Methods_of_contour_integration" title="en:Methods of contour integration"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Methods of contour integration</span></a></span>）</span></span>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.87.8F.E5.AD.90.E5.8A.9B.E5.AD.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="量子力學">量子力學</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="编辑章节：量子力學">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%87%8F%E5%AD%90%E5%8A%9B%E5%AD%B8" title="量子力學">量子力學</a>中複數是十分重要的，因其理論是建基於複數體上無限維的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E5%B0%94%E4%BC%AF%E7%89%B9%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="希尔伯特空间">希尔伯特空间</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.9B.B8.E5.B0.8D.E8.AB.96"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="相對論">相對論</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="编辑章节：相對論">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>如將時間變數視為虛數的話便可簡化一些<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%8B%B9%E7%BE%A9%E7%9B%B8%E5%B0%8D%E8%AB%96" title="狹義相對論">狹義</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%BB%A3%E7%BE%A9%E7%9B%B8%E5%B0%8D%E8%AB%96" title="廣義相對論">廣義相對論</a>中的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%99%82%E7%A9%BA" title="時空">時空</a>度量 (Metric)方程。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.87.89.E7.94.A8.E6.95.B8.E5.AD.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="應用數學">應用數學</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="编辑章节：應用數學">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>實際應用中，求解給定<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B7%AE%E5%88%86%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="差分方程">差分方程</a>模型的系統，通常首先找出線性差分方程對應的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="特征方程">特徵方程</a>的所有複特徵根<i>r</i>，再將系統以形爲<i>f</i>(<i>t</i>)= <i>e</i><sup><i>rt</i></sup>的基函數的線性組合表示。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.B5.81-.7Bzh-hans:.E4.BD.93.3B_zh-hant:.E9.AB.94.3B.7D-.E5.8A.9B.E5.AD.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="流-{zh-hans:体;_zh-hant:體;}-力學">流体力學</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="编辑章节：流体力學">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>複函數於<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B5%81%E9%AB%94%E5%8A%9B%E5%AD%B8" title="流體力學">流体力學</a>中可描述<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%8C%E7%B6%AD" title="二維">二維</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8A%BF%E6%B5%81" title="势流">勢流</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.88.86.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="分形">分形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="编辑章节：分形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>一些<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E5%BD%A2" title="分形">分形</a>如<a href="/wiki/%E6%9B%BC%E5%BE%B7%E5%8D%9A%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88" title="曼德博集合">曼德博集合</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8C%B9%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%9A%E9%9B%86" title="茹利亚集">茹利亚集</a>（Julia set）是建基於複平面上的點的。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.A4.8D.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.B9.B3.E6.96.B9.E6.A0.B9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="复数的平方根">复数的平方根</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="编辑章节：复数的平方根">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E6%A0%B9#负数与複數的平方根" title="平方根">平方根 § 负数与複數的平方根</a></div>
<p>复数的平方根是可以计算的。其公式为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {x+iy}}={\sqrt {\frac {\left|x+iy\right|+x}{2}}}\pm i{\sqrt {\frac {\left|x+iy\right|-x}{2}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.80.83.E8.B3.87.E6.96.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="參考資料">參考資料</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：參考資料">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span id=".E5.BB.B6.E4.BC.B8.E9.96.B1.E8.AE.80"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="延伸閱讀">延伸閱讀</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="编辑章节：延伸閱讀">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><i>An Imaginary Tale: The Story of <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {-1}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mn>1</mn>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {-1}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sqrt{-1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4ea1ea9ac61e6e1e84ac39130f78143c18865719" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.906ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span></i>, by Paul J. Nahin; Princeton University Press; <a class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn" href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/0691027951">ISBN 0-691-02795-1</a> (hardcover, 1998). A gentle introduction to the history of complex numbers and the beginnings of complex analysis.</li>
<li><i>Numbers</i>, by H.-D. Ebbinghaus, H. Hermes, F. Hirzebruch, M. Koecher, K. Mainzer, J. Neukirch, A. Prestel, R. Remmert; Springer; <a class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn" href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/0387974970">ISBN 0-387-97497-0</a> (hardcover, 1991). An advanced perspective on the historical development of the concept of number.</li>
<li><i>The Road to Reality: A Complete Guide to the Laws of the Universe</i>, by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Roger_Penrose" title="Roger Penrose">Roger Penrose</a>; Alfred A. Knopf, 2005; <a class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn" href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/0679454438">ISBN 0-679-45443-8</a>. Chapters 4-7 in particular deal extensively (and enthusiastically) with complex numbers.</li>
<li><i>Unknown Quantity: A Real and Imaginary History of Algebra</i>, by John Derbyshire; Joseph Henry Press; <a class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn" href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/030909657X">ISBN 0-309-09657-X</a> (hardcover 2006).  A very readable history with emphasis on solving polynomial equations and the structures of modern algebra.</li>
<li><i>Visual Complex Analysis</i>, by <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Tristan_Needham&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Tristan Needham（页面不存在）">Tristan Needham</a>; Clarendon Press; <a class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn" href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/0198534477">ISBN 0-19-853447-7</a> (hardcover, 1997). History of complex numbers and complex analysis with compelling and useful visual interpretations.</li></ul>
